Those who take revenge after they have suffered wrong, for such there is no way (of blame) against them
The way (of blame) is only against those who oppress people and rebel in the earth without right. It is they who will have a painful punishment
Surely, those who show patience and forgive, surely would be from the steadfast things
Those whom Allah sends astray, there is no protector for them after Him. When they will face the punishment, you will see the wrongdoers say: “Is there any way for return (to the world)?”
You will see them brought forward to it (hell) made humble by disgrace, looking with stealthy glance. Those who believe will say: “Surely, the losers are they who have lost themselves and their families on the Day of Resurrection. Surely, indeed the wrongdoers will be in a lasting punishment.”
They will not have any protector in it to help them other than Allah. The one whom Allah sends astray, there is no way of escape
Answer the call of your Lord before there comes from Allah a Day which cannot be averted. You will not have any refuge on that Day nor will you be able to deny (your misdeeds)
But if they turn away, (they should know that) We have not sent you (O Muhammad) over them as a guardian. Your duty is to convey (the message). Surely, when We cause people to taste the Mercy from Us, they rejoice in it; but when some ill befalls them because of (misdeeds) which their hands have sent forth, then surely, the people become ungrateful
To Allah belongs the kingdom of the heavens and the earth. He creates what He wills. He bestows female (daughter) to whom He wills and bestows male (son) to whom He wills
Or He combines them both males and females, and He renders barren whom He wills. Surely, He is the All-Knower of everything and is Able to do all things
It is not given to any human being that Allah should speak (directly) unless (it be) by inspiration, or from behind a veil, or by sending a Messenger to reveal by His permission what He wills. Surely, He is High, Wise
Thus We have sent to you (O Muhammad) a revelation (Qur’an) of Our command. You did not know what the book is or what the faith is! But We have made it (this Qur’an) a light, We guide by it whoever We will of Our servants. Surely, you (O Muhammad) are indeed guiding mankind to the Right Way
the way of Allah, to whom belongs all that is in the heavens and in the earth. Surely, all the matters return to Allah (for decision)
Ha-Mim
By the clear book (the Qur’an)
Surely, We surely has revealed it a Qur’an in Arabic so that you may be able to understand
And surely, it (this Qur’an) is in the mother of the book (Al-Lauh Al-Mahfooz) before US, indeed exalted, full of wisdom
Should We then take away the reminder (this Qur’an) from you in your rejection because you are a transgressing people
And how many prophets have We sent amongst the previous people
Never came to them a prophet and they did not mock at him
So We destroyed people stronger than them in power, and the example of the ancient people has passed away (before them)
Indeed if you (O Muhammad) ask them: “Who has created the heavens and the earth?” They will surely say: “The All-Mighty, the All-Knower of everything created them.”
(Allah) Who has made the earth like a bed for you and has made roads for you in it in order that you may find your way
and Who sends down water (rain) from the sky in due measure. Then We revive a dead land from it, and even so you will be brought out (from the dead again)
and Who has created all the pairs and has appointed for you from ships and cattle on which you ride
in order that you may mount firmly on their backs, and then may remember the Favor of your Lord when you mount on them, and say: “Glory to Allah who has subjected this to us, and we could never have ability for it (by our efforts)
and surely, to our Lord we all shall return.”
Yet they assign to some of His servants a share with Him (as partners). Surely, mankind is clearly ungrateful
Or has He taken daughters (pagan Arabs used to believe that angels were daughters of Allah) out of what He has created, and has He selected for you sons
Yet, if the news of one (the birth of a girl) of them is informed which it sets forth as a parable to the Beneficent (Allah), its face becomes dark, gloomy, and is filled with grief
(Do they then like for Allah) a creature who is brought up in ornaments (women) and is unable to make itself clear in dispute
And they regard the angels as females who themselves are servants of the beneficent (Allah). Did they witness their creation? Their witness will be recorded and they will be questioned
And they say: “If it had been the Will of the beneficent (Allah), we would not have worshipped them (false deities).” They don’t have any knowledge of that. They don’thing but lie
Or have We given them any book before this (the Qur’an) which they hold fast to it
Nay! They said: “We found our forefathers following on a certain way and religion, and we guide ourselves on their footsteps.”
And similarly, whenever We sent a Warner before you (O Muhammad) to any town (people), its luxurious people among them said: “We found our forefathers following on a certain way and religion, and we are indeed following their footsteps.”
(The Warner) said: “What if I bring you better guidance than that which you found your forefathers on it?” They said: “Surely, We disbelieve in it with which you have been sent.”
So We took retribution on them; and then see how the end of those who denied was
(Remember) when Abraham said to his father and his people: “Surely, I renounce (deities) that you worship
except Him (alone) who created me, and surely, He will guide me.”
And he made it a word lasting among his offspring so that they may turn back (to repent to Allah)
Nay, but I gave (good things) to these (polytheists) and their forefathers to enjoy (this life), till there came to them the truth (the Qur’an) and a Messenger (Muhammad) making things clear
And when the truth (this Qur’an) came to them, they (disbelievers) said: “This is magic, and we don’t believe in it.”
And they said: “Why is this Qur’an not sent down to some great man of the 2 towns (Makkah and Taif)?”
Is it they who would distribute the Mercy of your Lord? It is We Who distributes between them their livelihood in the life of this world, and We raise some of them above others in ranks, so that some may employ others in their work. The Mercy of your (O Muhammad) Lord is better than the (wealth of this world) which they accumulate
And were it not that all mankind would become one community (of disbelievers), We would have provided for those who disbelieve in the Beneficent (Allah), silver roofs for their houses, and elevators on which they mount
and doors (of silver) for their houses and thrones (of silver) on which they recline
and adornments of gold. Yet all these are nothing but an enjoyment of the life of this world. And the Hereafter is only for the pious which is with your Lord
And whoever turns away from the remembrance of the Beneficent (Allah), We appoint a Satan for it who becomes a companion for him
and surely, they (Satans) hinder them from the Way (of Allah) but they think that they are guided aright
Till, when such one comes to Us (on the Day of Judgment), it says (to its Satan): “I wish that between me and you were the distance of the 2 easts (or the east and west), you were an evil companion!”
(It will be said to them): “It will not profit you this Day as you already did wrong, and both of you will be sharing the punishment.”
Can you (O Muhammad) make the deaf to hear, or guide the blind or those who are in clear error
And even if We take you (O Muhammad) away, We shall indeed take retribution on them
or if We show you (the end of) what We have threatened them, then surely, We have perfect command over them
So you (O Muhammad) hold fast to that (the Qur’an) which is revealed to you. Surely, you are on a Right Way
And surely, this (the Qur’an) is indeed a reminder for you (O Muhammad), your people, and you will be questioned about it
And ask (O Muhammad) those of Our Messengers whom We sent before you: “Did We ever appoint any other one worthy of worship to be worshipped besides the Beneficent (Allah)?”
And indeed We sent Moses with Our Signs to Pharaoh and his chiefs (inviting them to Allah). He said: “Surely, I am a Messenger of the Lord of the worlds.”
When he came to them with Our Signs, behold! They laughed at them
Yet, We showed them sign after sign each greater than its preceding and We seized them with punishment in order that they might turn (to Right Way)
And then they said (to Moses): “O you sorcerer! Invoke your Lord for us according to what He has entrusted with you. Surely, We shall guide.”
But when We removed the punishment from them, behold! They broke their covenant
Then Pharaoh proclaimed amongst his people, saying: “O my people! Is not the dominion of Egypt mine? Are not these rivers flowing underneath me? Then don’t you see
Or am I not better than this one (Moses), who is despicable and can hardly express himself clearly
(If he is true Messenger) why then bracelets of gold are not bestowed on him, or angels sent along with him?”
Thus he (Pharaoh) befooled and misled his people, and they obeyed him. Surely, they were a people who were sinners
So when they angered Us, We punished them, and drowned them all
and We made them a precedent (a lesson for future), and an example to later generations
And when the son of Mary (Jesus) is quoted as an example (Jesus is worshipped like their idols), behold! Your people cry aloud about it
and say: “Are our deities better or is he (Jesus)?” They did not quote the above example for you except for argument. But they are a quarrelsome people
He (Jesus) was not more than a servant (of Allah). We granted Our Favor to him, and We made him an example to the children of Israel (created without a father)
And if it were Our Will, We would have (destroyed mankind and) made angels to replace you on the earth
And he (Jesus) is a known sign for the (coming of the) Hour (Day of Resurrection). Therefore, don’t have doubt concerning it (the Day of Resurrection). And follow Me! This is the Right Way
Let not Satan hinders you (from the right religion). Surely, he is your open enemy
When Jesus came with (Our) clear signs, he said: “Surely I have come to you with wisdom (Prophethood), and to clarify to you some of the points in which you differ, therefore fear Allah and obey me
Surely, it is He Who is my Lord and your Lord. So worship Him (alone). This is the Right Way.”
But the sects differed among themselves. So woe to the wrongdoers (who ascribe things to Jesus that are not true) from the punishment of the painful Day (of Resurrection)
Are they only waiting for the Hour that it will come on them suddenly, while they don’t perceive
On that Day, even friends will be enemies to one another accept the pious
(It will be said to the believers): “My worshippers! Today you have nothing to fear or to grieve
you are those who believed in Our Revelations and were Muslims
‘Enter Paradise, you and your wives in happiness.’”
Trays of gold and cups will be (used to) serve round them, there will be everything that the souls could desire, and all that their eyes can delight in, and (it will be said to them): “You will abide in it forever
This is the Paradise which you have made to inherit because of your good deeds which you used to do (in the world)
in it you will have plenty of fruits to eat.”
But the criminals will abide in the punishment of hell forever
(Their punishment) will not be lightened for them and they will be plunged into destruction with despair in it
We did not wrong them, but they were the wrongdoers
They will cry: “O Malik (keeper of hell)! Let your Lord put an end to us.” It will say: “Surely you shall abide forever.”
Indeed We have brought the truth (the Qur’an) to you, but most of you hate the truth
Or have they plotted some plan (against you O Muhammad)? Then We too are planning (to destroy them)
Or do they think that We don’t hear their secrets and their private counsel? Of course Our Messengers (angels) are recording by them
Say (O Muhammad): “If the Beneficent (Allah) (suppose) had a son, then I would be the first of worshippers.”
Glory be to the Lord of the heavens and the earth, the Lord of the Throne! (Exalted be He) above all that they ascribe (to Him)
So leave them alone to speak nonsense and play until they meet their Day, which they have been promised
It is He Who is to be worshipped in the heaven and to be worshipped on the earth. And He is the All-Wise, the All-Knower
And blessed be He to whom belongs the kingdom of the heavens and the earth and all that is between them. He (alone) has the knowledge of the Hour (of judgment), and to Whom you all will be returned
And those whom they invoke besides Him, has no power of intercession; except those who bear witness to the truth (believers), and they know (the facts about the Oneness of Allah)
And if you ask them who created them, they will surely say: “Allah.” How then are they turned away (from Allah)
(Allah has knowledge) of (Muhammad’s) saying: “O my Lord! Surely, these are a people who don’t believe!”
So turn away from them (O Muhammad), and say: Salam (peace)! They will come to know (the truth)
Ha-Mim
By the clear book (the Qur’an)
Surely We sent it (this Qur’an) down in a blessed night (of Qadr in the month of Ramadan). Surely, We are ever warning (mankind)
in it (that night) every matter is decided wisely
by a command from Us. Surely, We have ever sending (the Messengers)
(as) Mercy from your Lord. Surely! He is the All-Hearer, the All-Knower
The Lord of the heavens and the earth and all that is between them, if you have faith with certainty
There is no true one worthy of worship but He. It is He Who gives life and causes death, your Lord and the Lord of your forefathers
Nay! They play in doubt
Then you wait for the Day when the sky will bring forth a visible smoke
covering the people, this will be a painful punishment
(People will say): “Our Lord! Remove the punishment from us, really we have become believers!”
How can there be an admonition (at the time when the punishment has reached) for them when a Messenger explaining things clearly has already come to them
Yet, they turn away from him (Muhammad) and said: “He (Muhammad) is a madman, taught (by others)!”
Surely, We shall remove the punishment (famine) for a while. But you will return (to disbelief)
On the Day We shall seize you with the greatest grasp. Surely, We will take retribution
And indeed We tried Pharaoh’s people before them, when a noble Messenger (Moses) came to them
saying: “Deliver the servants of Allah (the children of Israel) to me. Surely! I am a Messenger to you worthy of all trust
And don’t exalt (yourselves) against Allah. Truly, I have come to you with a clear authority
And truly, I seek refuge in my Lord and your Lord, lest you stone me
But if you don’t believe me, then keep away from me and leave me alone.”
So he (Moses) called upon (when they were aggressive) his Lord (saying) indeed: “These are criminal people.”
(Allah said): “You depart with My servants by night. Surely, you will be pursued
And (when you have crossed the sea with your people), then leave the sea as it is (quiet and divided). Surely, they are a host to be drowned.”
How many gardens and springs did they (Pharaoh’s people) leave behind
and corn-fields and goodly places
and comforts (of life) they used to take delight in it
Thus We made other people inherit them (the children of Israel inherit the kingdom of Egypt)
And neither the heavens and the earth did weep for them, nor were they given a respite
And indeed We saved the children of Israel from the humiliating punishment
from Pharaoh. Surely! He was arrogant and was one of the transgressors
and surely, We chose them (the children of Israel) above the worlds (during the time of Moses) with knowledge
And granted them signs in which there was a plain trial
Surely, these (people of Quraish) say
“There is nothing after our first death and we shall not be resurrected
Bring back our forefathers if you speak the truth!”
Are they better than the people of Tubba and those who were before them? We destroyed them because they were indeed criminals
And We did not create the heavens and the earth, and all that is between them, for merely a play
We have not created them but (to reveal) the truth, but most of them don’t know
Surely, the Day of judgment is the time appointed for all of them
the Day when a near relative cannot avail a relative in anything, nor they can receive help
except those on whom Allah will show Mercy. Surely, He is the Mighty, the Merciful
Surely, the tree of Zaqqum (very bitter taste)
will be the food of the sinners
like boiling oil, it will boil in the bellies
like the boiling of scalding water
(It will be said): “Seize and drag him into the midst of blazing fire
then pour from the punishment of boiling water over its head
taste you (this)! Surely, you were (pretending to be) the mighty, the noble
Surely! This is what you used to doubt about it!”
Surely! The pious will be in place of security (Paradise)
among gardens and springs
dressed in fine silk and also in thick silk, facing each other
So (it will be), and We shall marry them to Houris (fair females) with wide lovely eyes
They will call in it for every kind of fruit in peace and security
they will never taste death in it except the first death (of this world), and He will save them from the punishment of the blazing fire
as a Bounty from your Lord! That will be the supreme success
Certainly, We have made this (Qur’an) easy in your tongue in order that they may remember
Wait then (O Muhammad); surely, they too are waiting
Ha-Mim
The revelation of the book (this Qur’an) is from Allah, the All-Mighty, the All-Wise
Surely, in the heavens and the earth there are signs for the believers
in your own creation and that of moving creatures which He has scattered (through the earth), there are signs for people who have firm faith
and in the alternation of the night and the day, in the provision that Allah sends down from the sky and revives with it the earth after its death and in the turning of the winds, there are signs for those people who understand
These are the revelations of Allah, which We recite to you (O Muhammad) with truth. Then in which report after Allah and His revelations, will they believe
Woe to every sinful liar
before whom the revelations of Allah are recited, yet persists with pride as if it did not hear them. So announce a painful punishment to them
And when one learns something of Our Revelations (this Qur’an), it takes them as a joke. For such people, there will be a humiliating punishment
In front of them there is hell, and nothing of what they have earned (in this world) will be of any benefit to them, nor those whom they have taken as protectors besides Allah. They will have a great punishment
This (Qur’an) is guidance. Those who disbelieve in the revelations of their Lord, there will be a terrible painful punishment for them
Allah, it is He Who has subjected the sea to you, so that the ships may sail through it by His Command, and that you may seek His Bounty and you may be thankful
and has subjected to you all that is in the heavens and all that is in the earth; all from Him. Surely, there are signs for those people who think deeply in it
Say (O Muhammad) to those who have believed, to forgive those who don’t hope for the (bad) days from Allah, so that He may recompense those people according to what they have earned
Whoever does a good deed, it is for its own self; and whoever does evil, it is against it (own self). Then you will be made to return to your Lord
And indeed We gave the Scripture to the children of Israel, the understanding of the Scripture, and the Prophethood, and provided them with good things of life, and preferred them above all the worlds (during that time)
and gave them clear proofs of matters (revealed in the Torah). They did not differ until after the knowledge had come to them, through transgression among themselves. Surely, Your Lord will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection about which they used to differ
Then We have put you (O Muhammad) on the plain Way of (Our) commandment. So follow it (Islam) and don’t follow the desires of those who don’t know
surely, they can avail you nothing against Allah. Surely, the wrongdoers are friends of one another, while Allah is the protector of the pious people
This (Qur’an) is a clear insight and evidence for mankind; guidance and a Mercy for those who have firm faith
Or do those evil doers think that We shall make them equal with those who believe and do righteous deeds, in their present life and after their death? Worst is the judgment that they make
And Allah has created the heavens and the earth with truth, in order that each person may be recompensed what it has earned, and none of them will be wronged
Have you seen the one who has taken its own desires as worthy of worship? And Allah lets it astray upon knowing, and sealed over its hearing and its heart, and put a cover on its sight. Who then will guide him after Allah (has withdrawn)? Will you not then remember
And they (disbelievers) say: “There is nothing but our life of this world. We die and we live, nothing but time destroys us.” They have no knowledge of it, verily they are only guessing
And when Our clear revelations are recited to them, their argument is not except that they say: “Bring back our dead forefathers if you are truthful!”
(O Muhammad) say (to them): “Allah gives you life and then causes you to die; then He will assemble you to the Day of Resurrection. There is no doubt about it. But most people don’t know.”
And to Allah belongs the kingdom of the heavens and the earth. On the Day when the Hour (of judgment) will be established, the followers of falsehood shall lose on that Day
And you will see every nation humbled to its knees. Each nation will be called to its Record (of deeds). (It will be said): “This Day you shall be recompensed for what you used to do
This Our record speaks about you with truth. Surely, We were recording (by angels) what you used to do.”
Then, as for those who believed and did righteous deeds, their Lord will admit them into His Mercy. That will be the clear success
But as for those who disbelieved (it will be said to them): “Were not Our Revelations recited to you? But you were proud and became a nation of criminals.”
And when it was said: “Surely! Allah’s Promise is true and there is no doubt about the Hour (of judgment).” You used to say: ‘We don’t know what is the Hour (of Judgment); we think it only as a guess, and we have no firm convincing belief.’”
And the evil of their deeds will appear to them and they will be completely encircled by that which they used to mock at
And it will be said: “This Day We will forget you as you forgot the meeting of this Day of yours. Your abode will be the fire, and there will be no helper for you
This is because you used to take the revelations of Allah (this Qur’an) as a joke and the life of the world deceived you.” So this Day neither they shall be taken out from there (hell), nor shall they be allowed excuses (to amend their ways to please Allah)
So all the praises and thanks are to Allah, the Lord of the heavens, the Lord of the earth, and the Lord of the worlds
And to Him belongs the Majesty in the heavens and the earth, and He is the All-Mighty, the All-Wise
Ha-Mim
The revelation of the book (this Qur’an) is from Allah, the All-Mighty, the All-Wise
We have not created the heavens and the earth and all that is between them except with truth, and for an appointed term. Those who disbelieve turn away from that where they are warned
Say (O Muhammad): “Do you see what you invoke besides Allah? Show me what have they created of the earth? Or do they have any share in (the creation of) the heavens? Bring me any book (revealed) before this or some trace of knowledge (to support your claims), if you are truthful!”
And who is more astray than one who calls (deities) besides Allah, one who will not answer till the Day of Resurrection, and who are not even aware of their calls to them
And when mankind shall be gathered (on the Day of Resurrection), they (false deities) will become enemies for them and will deny their worshipping
And when Our clear revelations are recited to them, and the truth (this Qur’an) reaches them, the disbelievers say: “This is plain magic!”
Or they say: “He (Muhammad) has fabricated it.” Say: “If I have fabricated it, then you have no power to support me in anything against (the Wrath of) Allah. He knows better of what you say among yourselves concerning it (this Qur’an)! He is sufficient as a witness between me and between you! And He is the Forgiving, the Merciful.”
Say (O Muhammad): “I am not a new thing among the Messengers (of Allah) and I don’t know what will be done with me or with you. I only follow what is revealed to me, and I am not but a plain Warner.”
Say: “Do you see, if this (Qur’an) is from Allah and you deny it, and a witness from the children of Israel (Abdullah bin Salam) has testified to its similarity (that this Qur’an is from Allah like the Torah), and he has believed (embraced Islam), while you are too proud (to believe). Surely! Allah does not guide the wrongdoers.”
And those who disbelieve (strong and wealthy) say to those who believe (weak and poor): “Had it (the Qur’an) been a good thing, they (believers) would not have believed in it before us!” Since they did not accept its guidance (this Qur’an), they say: “This is an ancient lie!”
And from before, this was the Scripture of Moses as a guide and a Mercy. This book (the Qur’an) confirms it. It is revealed in the Arabic language to warn those who do wrong, and as glad tidings to the righteous people
Surely, those who say: “Our Lord is (only) Allah,” and thereafter stand firm, there shall be no fear on them, nor they shall grieve
They shall be the residents of Paradise, abide in it forever, a reward for what they used to do
And We have enjoined on people to be dutiful and kind to their parents. Its mother bears it with hardships and she brings it forth with hardships, and the bearing of it, and the weaning of it is 30 months. Till when it attains full strength and reaches 40 years, it says: “My Lord! Grant me the power and ability so that I may be grateful for Your Favor which You have bestowed upon me and upon my parents, and that I may do righteous deeds such as to please You, and make my offspring good for me. Truly, I have turned to You in repentance, and truly, I am one of the Muslims.”
They are those from whom We shall accept the best of their deeds and overlook their evil deeds. They will be among the residents of Paradise, a Promise of truth which they have been promised
But one who says to its parents: “Uff upon you both! Do you hold out the promise to me that I shall be raised up again and surely generations before me have passed away (without rising)?” While they (father and mother) invoke Allah (for help and rebuke their son): “Woe to you! Believe! Surely, the Promise of Allah is true.” But he says: “This is nothing but the tales of the ancient.”
They are those against whom the word (of punishment) is justified and they will be among the previous generations of jinns and mankind that surely have passed away. Surely! They will be the losers
For all, there will be ranks according to their deed, so that He may recompense them fully for their deeds. They will not be wronged
On the Day when those who disbelieved will be exposed to the fire (it will be said): “You received your good things in the life of the world, and you took your pleasure in it. Now this Day you shall be recompensed with a punishment of humiliation because you were arrogant in the land without a right, and because you used to rebel and disobey (Allah).”
And remember (Hud) the brother of Ad, when he warned his people in the curved sand-hills (located in the southern part of Arabian Peninsula). Surely, warners have passed before him and after him (saying): “Worship none but Allah. Truly, I fear for you the punishment of a mighty Day.”
They said: “Have you come to us to turn us away from our deity? Then bring us that (punishment) with which you threaten us, if you are one of the truthful!”
He said: “The knowledge (of the time of its coming) is only with Allah. I convey to you what I have been sent herewith, but I see that you are ignorant people.”
Then, when they saw it (punishment) as a dense cloud coming towards their valleys, they said: “This cloud will bring us rain.” Nay, but it is that (punishment) which you were asking to be hastened! It is a wind in it is a painful punishment
It will destroy everything by the command of its Lord. So they became such that nothing could be seen except their (ruined) residences! Thus We did recompense the people who were criminals
And indeed We had firmly established them much better than We have established you (O Quraish of Makkah)! And We had assigned for them hearing, seeing, and hearts. But their hearing, seeing and their hearts availed them nothing since they used to deny the revelations of Allah, and they were completely encircled by that which they used to mock at
And indeed We have destroyed towns (populations) around you, and We have shown them in various ways the revelations so that they may return (to the truth)
Then why did those whom they had taken as deities besides Allah, as a way of approach (to Allah) not help them? Nay, but they (deities) vanished completely from them (where punishment came). Those were their lies and false inventions (before their destruction)
And (remember) when We have sent towards you (Muhammad) a party of the jinns, quietly listening to the Qur’an when they stood in the presence thereof, they said: “Listen in silence!” When it was finished, they returned to their people, as warners
They said: “O our people! Surely! We have listened to a book (this Qur’an) sent down after Moses, confirming what came before it, and it guides to the truth and to the Right Way (Islam)
O our people! Respond to Allah’s caller (Muhammad), and believe in him. He will forgive you from your sins and will save you from a painful punishment (hellfire)
And whoever does not respond to Allah’s caller, it cannot escape on earth, and there will not be protectors for it besides Allah (from His punishment). Those people are in clear error.”
Don’t they see that Allah, who created the heavens and the earth and was not tired by their creation, is Able to give life to the dead? Yes, surely He has power over all things
On the Day when those who disbelieve will be exposed to the fire, (it will be said): “Is this not the truth?” They will say: “Yes, by our Lord!” He will say: “Taste the punishment, because you used to disbelieve!”
Therefore be patient (O Muhammad) as endured by those Messengers of strong will and don’t haste about them (disbelievers). On the Day when they will see that (punishment) with which they are being threatened as if they had not stayed more than an Hour in a single day. (This Qur’an is sufficient as) a clear message. But shall anyone be destroyed except the people who are sinners
Those who disbelieve and hinder people from the Way of Allah, He will render their deeds vain
But those who believe, do righteous deeds, and believe in what is sent down to Muhammad, for it is the truth from their Lord, He will remove their sins from them, and will make their condition good
That is because those who disbelieve follow falsehood, while those who believe follow the truth from their Lord. Thus Allah does set forth their examples for mankind
So, when you meet (fight with) those who disbelieve, strike at their necks till you have killed and wounded many of them, then bind a bond firmly (and take them as captives). After the war lays down its burden, then either show generosity (free them without ransom), or ransom (to benefit Islam). But if Allah had willed, He could certainly have won over them. But (He adapted this way) in order to test some of you with others. Those who are killed in the Way of Allah, He will never let their deeds be lost
He will guide them and set their state right
and admit them to Paradise which He has made known to them
O you who believe! If you help (the Cause of) Allah, He will help you, and make your foothold firm
But those who disbelieve, there is destruction for them, and (Allah) will make their deeds vain
That is because they hate that which Allah has sent down (this Qur’an), so He has made their deeds fruitless
Have they not traveled through the earth and seen how was the end of those before them? Allah destroyed them completely and its likeness (similar fate waits) for the disbelievers
That is because Allah is the Protector of those who believe and the disbelievers have no protector
Certainly! Allah will admit those who believe and do righteous deeds, to gardens under which rivers flow (Paradise). While those who disbelieve, enjoy themselves (in worldly life) and eat as cattle eat, but the fire will be abode for them
And many towns were stronger in strength than your town (Makkah) (O Muhammad), which has driven you out, We have destroyed them. There was none to help them
Is the one who is on a clear proof from its Lord be compared to those for whom their evil deeds are beautified for them, while they follow their own lusts (evil desires)
The description of Paradise which has been Promised for those who fear is that there are rivers of water not stagnant in it, rivers of milk whose taste never changes, rivers of wine delicious to those who drink, and rivers of clarified honey. In it, they will have every kind of fruit, and forgiveness from their Lord. (Are these) like those who shall reside forever in the fire and be given to drink boiling water so that it cuts up their intestines
And among them there are some who listen to you (O Muhammad) till, when they go out from you, they say to those who have received knowledge: “What has he said just now?” Such are those Allah has sealed on their hearts and they follow their lusts (evil desires)
Those who accept guidance, He will increase their guidance and bestow on them their piety
Are they waiting for the Hour (of judgment) so that it should come upon them suddenly? But indeed some of its signs have already come and when it will actually be on them, then how can they benefit by their reminder
So know (O Muhammad) that there is no one worthy of worship but Allah, and ask forgiveness for your sins, and also for believing men and believing women. Allah knows your activities well and your resting place (homes)
Those who believe say: “Why is not a Surah (chapter of the Qur’an) sent down (to allow us to fight)? But when a decisive Surah is sent down and fighting (in Allah’s Cause) is mentioned in it, you will see those in whose hearts is a disease (of hypocrisy) looking at you with a look of one fainting to death. But it was better for them
Obedience (to Allah) and good words (are better for them). When the matter (preparation for fight) is resolved, then if they had been true to Allah, it would have been better for them
Would you might then, if you were given the authority, do mischief in the land, and sever your ties of kinship
Such are they whom Allah has cursed so that He has made them deaf and blinded their sight
Will they not then think deeply in the Qur’an? Or are there locks in their hearts
Surely, those who turn on their backs after the guidance has become clear, Satan has beautified for them (false hopes), and (Allah) has prolonged them (their age)
This is because they said to those who hate what Allah has sent down: “We will obey you in some matter,” but Allah knows their secrets
Then what will they do when the angels will take their souls at death, striking their faces and their backs
That is because they followed what angered Allah and hated what pleased Him. So He made their deeds wasted
Or do those in whose hearts is a disease (of hypocrisy) think that Allah will never bring to light their hidden ill-wills
If We willed, We could have shown them to you and you would have known them by their marks. But surely, you will know them by the tone of their speech! Allah knows all your deeds
And surely, We shall try you till We know those who strive hard (for Allah) and from you the patient ones, and We shall test your facts (whether lying or not)
Surely, those who disbelieve and hinder people from the Way of Allah, and oppose the Messenger after the guidance has been clearly shown to them, they will never hurt Allah in the least, but He will make their deeds fruitless
O you who believe! Obey Allah, and obey the Messenger (Muhammad) and don’t render vain your deeds
Surely, those who disbelieve, and hinder people from the Way of Allah, then die while they are disbelievers; Allah will never forgive them
So don’t be weak and ask for peace while you have upper hand. Allah is with you, and will never decrease the reward of your good deeds
The life of this world is but play and pastime. But if you believe and fear Allah, and avoid evil, He will grant you your wages, and will not ask you your wealth
If He were to ask you of it, and press you, you would withhold with extreme desire, and He will bring out all your ill-wills
Behold! You are those who are called to spend in the Cause of Allah. Yet among you are some who are stingy. Whoever is stingy, and then one is stingy only to one’s own self. But Allah is Rich, and you people are poor. If you turn away (from the obedience of Allah), He will exchange you by some other people besides you who will not be like you
Surely, Allah has given to you (O Muhammad) a clear victory (treaty of Hudaibiyah)
so that Allah may forgive your past as well as future sins, complete His Favor on you, and guide you to the Right Way
and Allah may offer you with strong help
It is He Who has sent down the tranquility into the hearts of the believers so that they may add more faith to their present faith. And to Allah belong the forces of the heavens and the earth. Allah is the All-Knower, the All-Wise
(For good deeds) He may admit the believing men and the believing women to gardens under which rivers flow (Paradise), to abide in it forever and to compensate them from their sins, and that is the supreme success with Allah
and He may punish the hypocritical men and women, and also the polytheist men and women, who thought evil thoughts about Allah. For them there is a disgraceful punishment and the anger of Allah is upon them. He has cursed them, prepared hell for them, and worst indeed is that destination
And to Allah belong the forces of the heavens and the earth. And Allah is the All-Powerful, the All-Wise
Surely, We have sent you (O Muhammad) as a witness, as a bearer of glad tidings, and as a Warner
so that you people may believe in Allah and His Messenger, and that you may assist him, honor him, and glorify (Allah’s) praises morning and afternoon
Surely, those who gave allegiance to you (O Muhammad), indeed they gave allegiance to Allah. The authority of Allah was over their hands. Then whoever will break its pledge, will break only its own, and whoever will fulfill what it has pledged with Allah, He will bestow a great reward to it
Those of the Bedouins who stayed behind will say to you: “Our possessions and our families occupied us, so ask forgiveness for us.” They say with their tongues what is not in their hearts. Say: “Who then has any power (to intervene) on your behalf with Allah, if He intends to hurt you or intends to benefit you? Nay, but Allah is All-Aware of what you do
Nay, but you thought that the Messenger and the believers would never return to their families; and that was made seem fair in their hearts. You thought evil thoughts and you became a useless people for destruction.”
Whoever does not believe in Allah and His Messenger (Muhammad), then surely, We have prepared a blazing fire for the disbelievers
And to Allah belongs the sovereignty of the heavens and the earth, He forgives whom He wills, and punishes whom He wills. And Allah is ever Forgiving, Merciful
When you set forth to take them to the spoils (of war), those who stayed behind will say: “Allow us to follow you.” They want to change Allah’s Words. Say: “You shall not follow us. Allah has said this before.” They will say: “Nay, you envy us.” But they don’t understand except a little
Say (O Muhammad) to the Bedouins who stayed behind: “You shall be called to fight against a people with great warfare, then either you will fight them or they shall surrender. Then if you obey, Allah will give you a good reward, but if you turn away as you did turn away before, He will punish you with a painful punishment.”
There is no blame or sin on the blind, nor there is blame or sin on the lame, nor there is blame or sin on the sick (excused not to go to war). Whoever obeys Allah and His Messenger (Muhammad), He will admit to gardens beneath which rivers flow (Paradise); and whoever turns back, He will punish with a painful punishment
Indeed, Allah was pleased with the believers when they gave the allegiance to you (O Muhammad) under the tree. He knew what was in their hearts, He sent down the tranquility upon them, and He rewarded them with a near victory
and abundant spoils which they will capture. And Allah is All-Mighty, All-Wise
Allah has Promised you abundant spoils which you will capture, and He has hastened these (spoils of Khaibar) for you. He has restrained the hands of people (enemy) from you so that it may be a sign for the believers and that He may guide you to the Right Way
And others (victories and booty Promised) which are not yet within your power over it, indeed Allah has compassed them. And Allah has power over all things
If those who disbelieve fight against you, they would have turned their backs, and then they would have found neither a protector nor a helper
That has been the Way of Allah which already passed away before. You will never find any change in the Way of Allah
And it is He Who has restrained their hands from you and your hands from them in the midst of Makkah (through the peace treaty of Hudaibiyah), after that He had made you victors over them. And Allah is the All-Seer of what you do
They are the ones who disbelieved and obstructed you from the sacred Masjid (of Makkah) and detained the sacrificed animals from reaching their place of sacrifice. Had there not been believing men and believing women (in Makkah) whom you did not know, and you may trample (heavily burst) them under your feet and thus incurring a sin committed by you without your knowledge (but Allah held back your hands), so that Allah may admit to His Mercy whom He wills. If they (believers and disbelievers) should have been apart, We would have punished those of them who disbelieved with painful punishment
When those who disbelieve had put in their hearts pride and arrogance, the pride and arrogance of the time of ignorance, then Allah sent down His Tranquility upon His Messenger and upon the believers, and made them stick to the word of piety, and they were well entitled to it and worthy of it. And Allah is the All-Knower of everything
Indeed Allah will fulfill His Messenger’s true vision (which Allah showed him) in all truth. Certainly, you shall enter the sacred Masjid; if Allah wills, secure (to perform Umrah) having your heads shaved, and having your head hair cut short, having no fear. He knows what you don’t know, and besides He granted a near victory
It is He Who has sent His Messenger (Muhammad) with guidance and the religion of truth (Islam), so that He may make it (Islam) superior over all other religions. And Allah is All-Sufficient as a Witness
Muhammad is the Messenger of Allah, and those who are with him are strong against disbelievers, and merciful among themselves. You see them bowing and falling down prostrate (in prayer), seeking Bounty from Allah and (His) good pleasure. The mark of them (their faith) is on their faces (foreheads) from the traces of prostration. This is their description in the Torah. Their description in the Gospel is like a seed which sends forth its shoot, then makes it strong, it then becomes thick, and it stands right on its stem delighting the sowers (of the seed) so that He may make the disbelievers angry with them. Those among them who believe and do righteous deeds, Allah has Promised forgiveness and a great reward
O you who believe! Don’t put forward (your decision in advance) before Allah and His Messenger, and fear Allah. Surely! Allah is All-Hearer, All-Knower (of everything)
O you who believe! Don’t raise your voices above the voice of the prophet, nor speak aloud when talking to him as some of you speak aloud to one another, lest your deeds should become fruitless while you don’t perceive
Surely! Those who lower their voices in the presence of Allah’s Messenger, they are the ones whose hearts Allah has tested for piety. They shall have forgiveness and a great reward
Surely! Those who call you (O Muhammad) from behind the residences, most of them have no common sense
If they had patience until you could come out to them, it would certainly be better for them. Allah is Forgiving, Merciful
O you who believe! If a rebellious evil person comes to you with news, verify it, lest you should harm people in ignorance and afterwards you become regretful for what you have done
Know that the Messenger of Allah is among you. If he were to follow you (opinions and desires) in most of the affairs, you would surely be in trouble. Allah has made the faith beloved to you and beautified it in your hearts, and has made disbelief, wickedness and disobedience (to Allah and His Messenger) hateful to you. Such are they who are rightly guided
(through) a grace from Allah and His Favor. And Allah is All-Knower, All-Wise
And if 2 parties among the believers begin fighting, then make peace between them. But if one of them transgresses against the other, then you fight against the one who has transgressed until it complies with the command of Allah. Then if it complies, make reconciliation between them justly and be fair. Surely! Allah loves those who are just and fair
The believers are only brothers (in Islam). So make reconciliation between your brothers and fear Allah, so that you may receive mercy
O you who believe! Let not a group mock at another group, it may be that the latter are better than them (former). Nor let (some) women mock at other women, it may be that they (latter) are better than them (former), nor defame one another, nor insult one another by nicknames. How bad is it (to call) wicked name after having faith. Whoever does not repent, then such are indeed wrongdoers
O you who believe! Avoid much of suspicions, indeed some suspicions are sins. Don’t spy, nor backbite some of you to others. Would one of you like to eat the flesh of its dead brother? You would hate it. Fear Allah. Surely, Allah is the one who Accepts repentance, Merciful
O mankind! Surely We have created you from a male and a female, and made you into nations and tribes so that you may know one another. Surely, the most honorable of you with Allah is the most pious of you. Surely, Allah is All-Knower, All-Aware
The Bedouins say: "We believe." Say: "You don’t believe but you only say, we have submitted (in Islam), for the faith has not yet entered into your hearts. But if you obey Allah and His Messenger, He will not decrease anything in reward for your deeds. Surely, Allah is Forgiving, Merciful
Only those are the believers who believe in Allah and His Messenger, and afterward don’t doubt but they strive with their wealth and their lives in the Way of Allah. They are those who are truthful
Say (O Muhammad): "Will you inform Allah about your religion? Allah knows all that is in the heavens and all that is in the earth, and Allah is All-Aware of everything
They regard as favor upon you (O Muhammad) that they have embraced Islam. Say: "Don’t count your Islam as a favor upon me. Nay, but Allah has conferred a favor upon you that Allah has guided you to the faith; (agree) if you indeed are truthful
Surely, Allah knows the unseen of the heavens and the earth. Allah is the All-Seer of what you do
Qaf. By the Glorious Qur’an
But they wonder that there has come to them a Warner (Muhammad) from among themselves. So the disbelievers say: “This is a strange thing
that after we are dead and have become dust (we shall be resurrected), that is a far return.”
Indeed We know that the earth consumes them (their dead bodies) and with Us there is a book preserved (with all records)
Nay, but they deny the truth (this Qur’an) when it comes to them, so they are confused (can not differentiate between right and wrong)
Have they not looked at the sky above them, (and see) how We have made it, adorned it, and there are no flaws in it
And the earth! We have spread it out, set on it mountains standing firm, and has produced every kind of lovely growth (plants) in it
(All these are) an insight and a reminder for every servant turning to Allah
And We send down blessed water (rain) from the sky, then We produce with it gardens and grain (crops) that are reaped
and tall date-palms with arranged clusters (of dates)
and provision for (Allah’s) servants. Thus We give life to a dead land with it. That is how the Resurrection (of the dead) will be
Denied before them (the pagans of Makkah) the people of Noah, the residents of Al-Rass, and the Thamud
and Ad, Pharaoh, and the brothers of Lot
the residents of the Al-Aiykah (wood), and the people of Tubba; every one of them denied Messengers, so My threat took effect (upon them)
Were We tired with the first creation? Nay, they are in confused doubt about a new creation (Resurrection)
And indeed We have created mankind and We know what one’s own self whispers to it. And We are nearer to one than rope of its jugular vein (by Our knowledge)
(Remember!) that the 2 receivers (recording angels) receive (for each human) sitting on the right and on the left (to record actions)
not a word does one utter but there is a watcher by it ready (to record)
And when the agony of death will come in truth (they will say): “This is what you were trying to avoid from it!”
And the trumpet will be blown; that will be the Day of warning (Resurrection)
And every person will come forth along with an (angel) to drive, and an (angel) to bear witness
(It will be said to the sinners): “Indeed you were heedless of this, but now We have removed your covering from you, and your eyesight is sharp this Day!”
And its companion (angel) will say: “Here is (record) ready with me!”
(It will be said): “Both of you (2 angels) throw every stubborn disbeliever into hell
opponent of good, doubting transgressor
who set up another one worthy of worship with Allah. So (both of you) cast him into the severe punishment.”
Its companion (Satan) will say: “Our Lord! I did not push him to transgress but he himself was in error far astray.”
(Allah) will say: “Don’t dispute in front of Me and surely I sent forth the threat (in advance) to you
The words from Me cannot be changed and I am not unjust to the servants.”
On that Day when We will ask the hell: “Are you filled?” It will say: “Are there any more (to come)?”
The Paradise will be brought near to the pious, which will not be far off
(it will be said): “This is what you were Promised. It is for every one returning (to Allah) in sincere repentance and those who preserve (their covenant with Allah)
who feared the Gracious (Allah) in the unseen (in the world) and brought a heart turned in repentance (to Him).”
(Allah will say): “You enter in it in peace and security; this is the Day of eternal life!”
They will have all that they desire in it, and We have more (for them)
And how many generations We have destroyed before them who were stronger in power than them? (When punishment came) they ran for a refuge in the land! Could they find any place of refuge (to save them from destruction)
Surely, in that, there is a lesson for one who has a heart or gives ear while one is witness
And indeed We created the heavens and the earth and all between them in 6 days, and no fatigue touched Allah
So, bear with patience (O Muhammad) on all that they say, and glorify the praises of your Lord before sunrise and before sunset
And during a part of the night, glorify His praises and after the prostration (prayers)
And listen on the Day when the caller will call from a near place
the Day when the people will hear the cry in truth; that will be the Day of coming out (dead will rise from the graves i.e., the Day of Resurrection)
Surely, it is We Who gives life and causes death; and to Us is the final return
on the Day when the earth shall be split asunder and the people will be rushing out of it; that will be a gathering quite easy for Us
We know very well what they (disbelievers) say. You (O Muhammad) are not a tyrant over them (to force them to believe). So warn by the Qur’an, (everyone) who fears My warning
By (the winds) that scatter dust
and (the clouds) that bear heavy weight of water
and (the ships) that float with ease and gentleness
and those (angels) that distribute command (of Allah)
surely that which you are Promised is true
and surely, the recompense is sure to happen
By the sky full of orbits
certainly, you have different ideas
turn aside from (Muhammad and the Qur’an) is the one who is turned aside
Curse be to the liars
who are under a cover of heedlessness (don’t think about the Hereafter)
They ask: “When will be the Day of recompense?”
(It will be) a Day when they will be punished over the fire
(it will be said): “You taste your trial (burning)! This is what you used to ask to be hastened!”
Surely, the pious will be in the midst of gardens and springs (in Paradise)
taking joy in the things which their Lord has given them. Surely, they were before this (in the world) righteous people
They used to sleep but little by the night
and ask (Allah) for forgiveness in the Hours before dawn
and share their properties with the needy (who asked) for it, and the deprived (who did not ask)
And in the earth, there are signs for those who have firm faith
and also in your own selves. Can you not then see
And in the heaven is your provision, and all that which you are Promised
Then by the Lord of the heaven and the earth, surely it is the truth just as what you speak
Has the story of the honored guests (angel Gabriel with 2 more angels) of Abraham reached you
When they came to him, and said: “Peace be upon you!” He answered: “Peace be upon you,” and said: “You are people unknown to me,”
then he turned to his family, brought out a fat roasted calf
and he put it before them (saying): “Will you not eat?”
(When they did not eat), he became afraid of them. They said: “Don’t fear.” They gave him glad tidings of an intelligent son
Then his wife came forward with a loud voice, she strikes her face and said: “(A son to) a barren old woman!”
They said: “Even so says your Lord. Surely, He is the All-Wise, the All-Knower.”
He (Abraham) said: “For what purpose you have come, O Messengers?”
They said: “We have been sent to a criminal people (of prophet Lot, who were homosexuals)
to send down upon them stones of baked clay
marked by your Lord for those who transgress Allah’s limits.”
So We brought out all those who were believers in the town
but We found none in it except one household of the Muslims (Lot and his 2 daughters)
and We left in it a sign (the Dead Sea in Palestine) for those who fear the painful punishment
And (There is sign in the story) of Moses, when We sent him to Pharaoh with a clear authority
but he (Pharaoh) turned away (from belief) with his hosts and said: “A sorcerer, or a madman.”
So, We took him and his hosts, and dumped them into the sea. Indeed he deserved to be blamed
(There is sign in the story) of Ad, when We sent against them the barren wind
which spared nothing that it reached and it blew on like something rotten (decayed)
And (there is sign in the story) of Thamud, when it was said to them: “Enjoy yourselves for a while (3 days),”
but they disobeyed the command of their Lord with arrogance; so the awful cry overtook them while they were looking
So neither they were able to rise up nor could they help themselves
(Allah destroyed) the people of Noah before them. Surely, they were people who were rebellious, disobedient (to Allah)
Allah has built the heaven with power. Surely, We are Able to extend the vastness of space in it
And We have spread out the earth, how Excellent Spreader are We
We have created everything in pairs, so that you may remember (Allah)
(Say to mankind, O Muhammad):“Rush towards Allah, surely, I (Muhammad) am from Him a plain Warner to you
And don’t set up any other one worthy of worship with Allah. Surely, I (Muhammad) am from Him a plain Warner to you.”
Likewise, whenever a Messenger came to those before them, they said: “A sorcerer or a madman!”
Have they (past people) transmitted this saying (to these pagans)? Nay, but they are a people transgressing beyond bounds
So, turn away (O Muhammad) from them (pagans), you are not to be blamed (you have conveyed message)
And remind (by preaching the Qur’an, O Muhammad), for surely, the reminding benefits the believers
I have not created the jinns and mankind except to worship Me (alone)
I don’t want any provision from them nor do I want that they feed Me
Surely, Allah is the All-Provider, Owner of Power, the Strong
And surely, for those who do wrong, there is a portion of punishment similar to the portion of the punishment of their friends (predecessors), so ask Me not to hasten on
Then, woe to those who disbelieve from their Day which they have been promised (for punishment)
By the (mount) Tur (where Moses received Torah)
and by the book inscribed
in parchment (written sheep skin) unrolled
and by the house (Bait-ul-Mamoor, the house over the heavens parallel to the Ka’bah at Makkah, visited by the angels)
and by the roof raised high (sky)
and by the sea boiling blaze
surely, the punishment of your Lord will surely come to pass
There is none that can avert it
On the Day when the heaven will shake with a dreadful shaking
and the mountains will move away with a horrible movement
On that Day, woe be to the rejecters (of truth)
who are engaged in falsehood
That Day they will be pushed down by force to the fire of hell with a forceful pushing
(it will be said to them): “This is the fire which you used to deny
Is this a magic, or do you not see
You burn in its heat; it will be the same for you whether you be patient or not be patient. You are only being requited for what you used to do.”
Surely, the pious will be in gardens (Paradise), and delight
enjoying in that which their Lord has bestowed on them and their Lord saved them from the punishment of the blazing fire
(It will be said to them): “Eat and drink with happiness because of what you used to do (good deeds).”
They will recline (with ease) on thrones arranged in ranks. And We shall marry them to lovely maidens with wide lovely eyes
Those who believe and their offspring follow them in faith, We will join their offspring to them, and We will not decrease any reward for their deeds. Every person has a pledge for that which it has earned
And We shall provide them with fruit and meat as they desire
They shall pass from hand to hand a wine cup in it which shall cause no dirty, false talk in it (between them), and no sin will go around
and boy-servants will go round for them to serve them as if they were preserved pearls
And some of them will come near to others, questioning (worldly life)
and they will say: “Surely, we were previously afraid with our families (from the punishment of Allah)
But Allah has been Gracious to us, and has saved us from the punishment of the fire
Surely, we used to invoke Him before. Surely, He is the Kind, the Merciful.”
Therefore, remind and preach (mankind, O Muhammad). By the Grace of Allah, you are neither a fortune-teller, nor a madman
Or do they say: “(Muhammad is) a poet! We are waiting for him some calamity (by time)!”
Say (O Muhammad to them): “Wait! I am with you among the waiters!”
Or do their minds command them this (to tell a lie against you)? Or are they people exceeding all bounds (from belief to disbelief)
Or do they say: “He (Muhammad) has forged it (this Qur’an)?” Nay! They don’t believe
Then let them produce a Scripture like it (the Qur’an) if they are truthful
Or were they created by no one? Or were they (themselves) the creators
Or have they created the heavens and the earth? Nay, but they have no firm belief
Or are the treasures of your Lord with them? Or are they the tyrants with the authority to do as they like
Or do they have a stairway (to heaven), by means of which they listen (to the talks of the angels)? Then let their listener produce some clear proof
Or has He only daughters and you have sons
Or is it that you (O Muhammad) ask a wage from them (for your preaching) so that they are burdened from a load of debt
Or is the (knowledge of) unseen with them and they write it down
Or do they intend a plot (against you)? If so, those who disbelieve are themselves (trapped) in a plot
Or do they have one worthy of worship other than Allah? Glorified is Allah from all that they ascribe as partners (to Him)
Even if they were to see a piece of the heaven falling down, they would say: “Clouds gathered in heaps!”
So leave them alone till they meet their Day, in which they will sink into a fainting (with horror)
The Day when their plotting will avail them nothing nor will be helped
Surely, for those who do wrong, there is punishment (in this world and in graves) before this, but most of them don’t know
So wait patiently (O Muhammad) for the decision of your Lord, for surely He is watching you. Glorify the praises of your Lord when you get up from sleep
and also glorify His praises in the night-time, and at the setting of stars
By the star when it goes down (vanishes)
your companion (Muhammad) has neither gone astray nor misguided
nor does he speak of (his own) desire
It is only a revelation that is revealed
He (Muhammad) has been taught (this Qur’an) by one mighty in power (angel Gabriel)
the one free from any defect who rose and became stable (in view)
While he (Gabriel) was in the highest part of the horizon
then he (Gabriel) approached and came closer
and was at a distance of 2 bow’s length or even closer
so he (Gabriel) conveyed the revelation to His servant (Muhammad) what he was supposed to reveal
(The prophet’s) heart did not deny what he (Muhammad) saw
Will you (disbelievers) then dispute with him (Muhammad) about what he saw (during his ascent journey over the 7 heavens)
Indeed he (Muhammad) saw him (Gabriel) another descent time
near Sidra-tul-Muntaha (the lote-tree at the farthest end of the 7th heavens, beyond which none can cross)
Near it is Jannatul-M’awa (the rest-house of Paradise)
When that lote-tree was covered with what covered it
the sight (of Muhammad) did not turn aside (right or left), nor it transgressed beyond limit
Indeed he (Muhammad) did see some of the greatest signs of his Lord
Have you then considered Lat, Uzza (2 idols of the pagan Arabs)
and another idol (Manat of the pagan Arabs), the other 3rd (as the daughters of Allah)
Is it for you the sons and for Him the daughters
This indeed is a division most unfair
They (Lat, Uzza, Manat) are nothing but names which you and your forefathers have named, for Allah has not sent down any authority in them. They (disbelievers) follow nothing but a guess which is their soul’s desire, even though the guidance has come to them from their Lord
Or should human have whatever he wishes
But to Allah belong the last (Hereafter) and the first (the world)
How many angels are there in the heavens; yet their intercession can avail nothing except what Allah gives permission for whom He wills and pleases
Surely those who don’t believe in the Hereafter, name the angels with female names
But they have no knowledge of it. They follow but a guess; and surely guess does not substitute for the truth at all
Therefore, withdraw (O Muhammad) from those who turn away from Our reminder (this Qur’an) and they only desire the life of this world
This is their highest point of knowledge. Surely, your Lord is He Who knows those best who go astray from His Way, and He knows those best who receive guidance
And to Allah belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is in the earth, so that He may requite those who do evil with what they have done (punish them in hell), and reward those who do good with what is best (Paradise)
Those who avoid major sins and shameful deeds except the small faults; surely, for them your Lord will have abundant forgiveness. He knew you well when He created you from the earth and when you were fetuses in your mother’s wombs. So don’t scribe piety to yourselves. He knows best who fears (Him)
Have you (O Muhammad) seen the one who (Waleed bin Mugheerah, who wanted to accept Islam but someone Promised him to take the punishment on his behalf for certain amount of money, he) turned away (from Islam)
He gave a little (amount of money), then he stopped (giving)
Does he has the knowledge of the unseen so that he sees (the reality)
Or has he not been informed about what was in the pages (Scripture) of Moses
and of Abraham who fulfilled (his covenant)
“That no burdened person (with sins) shall bear the burden of another
that a human can have nothing except what he strives for
that one’s efforts will be seen (checked)
that one will be fully recompensed and the best recompense
that to your Lord is the end
that it is He Who makes laugh and makes weep
that it is He Who causes death and gives life
that it is He Who created in pairs, the male and the female
from a drop of semen when it is emitted
that it is upon Him to grant another life (Resurrection)
that it is He Who gives much or little (of wealth and contentment)
that it is He the Lord of Sirius (the star whom the pagan Arabs used to worship)
and that it is He Who destroyed the former Ad (people)
and Thamud (people). So He spared none
and the people of Noah previously, surely they were more unjust and more rebellious and transgressing
And He destroyed the overthrown cities (of Sodom and Gomorrah during prophet Lot)
who were covered by (the punishment with stones) that covered them.”
Then which of the graces of your Lord will you doubt
This (Muhammad) is a Warner just like the old warners
The Day of Resurrection is drawing near
none besides Allah can avert it
Do you then wonder at this recital (the Qur’an)
and laugh at it and don’t weep
You are wasting your precious life in pastime and amusements
So you fall down in prostration to Allah and worship Him
The Hour (of doom) is drawing near, and the moon has split asunder (the people of Makkah requested Muhammad to show a miracle, so he showed them the splitting of the moon)
Yet, when they (disbelievers) see a sign, they turn away and say: “This is continuous magic.”
They deny (the Verses of this Qur’an) and follow their own lusts. Every matter will be settled (good deeds will take to Paradise, and evil deeds will take to hell)
And indeed there has come to them the news (in this Qur’an about previous nations) wherein there is (enough warning) to check (from evil)
perfect wisdom (as a warning), but (preaching of) warners don’t benefit them
So you (O Muhammad) withdraw from them. The Day when the caller will call them to a terrible thing
They will come out from their graves with their humbled eyes as if they were locusts spread abroad
rushing towards the caller and disbelievers will say: “This is a hard Day.”
The people of Noah denied (their Messenger) before them. They rejected Our servant and said: “A madman!” and he was rudely rebuked and threatened
(After warning people for 950 years) he invoked his Lord (saying): “I have been overcome, so help me!”
So We opened the gates of heaven with water (rain) pouring out
and We caused the earth to gush out with springs. So the waters met for a matter predestined
And We carried him on (a ship) built with planks and nails
floating under Our care, a reward for him (Noah) who was rejected (by disbelievers)
And indeed, We have left this (ship) as a sign, so is there any who will remember (or take admonition)
Then how terrible was My punishment and My warnings
And We have indeed made the Qur’an easy to understand and remember, and is there any who will remember (or take admonition)
Ad (people) denied (their Prophet Hud), then how terrible was My punishment and My warnings
Surely, We sent against them a furious wind of harsh voice on a Day of evil sign and continuous calamity
snatching out the people as if they were uprooted stems of date-palms
Then how terrible was My punishment and My warnings
And indeed We have made the Qur’an easy to understand and remember, then is there anyone who will remember (or take admonition)
Thamud (people) denied the warnings
they said: “A human alone from among us whom we are to follow? Truly, then we should be in error and madness
Is it that the reminder is sent only to him (prophet Saleh) from among us? Nay, he is an insolent liar!”
(Allah said to Saleh): “Tomorrow they will come to know, who the insolent liar is
Surely, We are sending the she-camel as a test for them. So watch them (O Saleh) and be patient
Inform them that the water is to be shared between them (and she-camel). Each (one’s right) to drink is being established (by turns)
But they (people of Thamud) called one of their comrades who took (responsibility) and killed (she-camel)
Then how terrible was My punishment and My warnings
Surely, We sent against them a single punishment (awful cry) and they became like the dry stubble (crushed twigs) of a fence-builder
And indeed, We have made the Qur’an easy to understand and remember, and is there any who will remember (or take admonition)
The people of Lot denied the warnings
Surely, We sent against them a storm of stones (which destroyed them), except the family of Lot, whom We saved in the last Hour of the night
as a Favor from Us. Thus We do reward those who give thanks (by obeying Us)
And indeed he (Lot) had warned them of Our grasp but they doubted the warnings
And indeed they even sought to lure him about his guest (by asking to commit sodomy with them). So We blinded their eyes and said: “Now you taste My punishment and My warnings.”
And surely, a lasting punishment seized them early in the morning
(as if to say): “Now you taste My punishment and My warnings.”
And indeed, We have made the Qur’an easy to understand and remember, and is there any who will remember (or take admonition)
And indeed, the warnings came to the people of Pharaoh (through Moses and Aaron)
(They) denied Our all signs. So We seized them with a seizure of the All-Mighty, All-Capable
Are your disbelievers (O Quraish!) better than these (nations of Noah, Lot, Saleh, and the people of Pharaoh who were destroyed)? Or have you granted immunity (against Our punishment) in the divine Scriptures
Or do they say: “We are great in numbers, and we shall be victorious?”
Their huge number will be put to flight, and they will show their backs
Nay, but the Hour is their appointed time (for recompense), and the Hour will be more grievous and more bitter
Surely, the criminals are in error (in this world) and will burn (in the hell in the Hereafter)
The Day when they will be dragged into the fire with their faces downwards, (it will be said to them): “You taste the touch of hell!”
Surely, We have created all things with divine ordainment
And Our Commandment is but one as the twinkling of an eye
And indeed, (O disbelievers) We have destroyed many like you, and is there any who will remember (or take admonition)
Each and everything they have done is being noted in their deed records
Everything, small and big, is being written down
Surely, the pious will be in the midst of gardens and rivers (Paradise)
in a seat of truth (Paradise), near the most Powerful King (Allah)
The Gracious (Allah)
Who taught (mankind) the Qur’an
created human
and taught human persuasive speech
The sun and the moon (run on their fixed courses) for reckoning
The stars and the trees both prostrate
And He has raised the heaven high, and He has set up the balance
so that you may not transgress in the balance
Establish the weight with justice and don’t give less in measurement
And He has put the earth for the creatures
therein are fruits, date-palms with sheathed fruit-stalks
and corn with leaves and stalk for food and sweet-scented plants
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
He created man from sounding clay like the clay of pottery
and He created the jinns from smokeless flame of fire
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
(He is) the Lord of the 2 easts (places of sunrise during summer and winter) and the Lord of the 2 wests (places of sunset during summer and winter)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
He has let loose the 2 seas (salt water and sweet water) meeting together
Yet, between them is a barrier which none of them can transgress
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Both pearl and coral come out of them
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
And the ships are His going and coming in the seas like mountains
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Everyone who is on it (earth) will perish
and the Face (authority) of your Lord will remain full of Majesty and Honor forever
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Whoever is in the heavens and on earth begs of Him (for needs). Every day He is engaged in some matter (task)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
We shall attend to you (give account), O you 2 classes (jinns and mankind)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
O assembly of jinns and mankind! If you have the power to pass beyond the zones of the heavens and the earth (to escape punishment), then pass them! But you will never be able to pass them, except with authority (from Allah)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
The smokeless flames of fire and molten brass will be sent against you both (jinns and mankind), and you will not be able to defend yourselves
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
When the heaven will burst and it becomes rosy (or red) like red hide
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
On that Day neither human nor jinn will be asked about their sins (their faces will be either white (for Paradise) or black (for hell)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
The sinners will be recognized by their marks (black faces) and they will be seized by their forelocks and their feet
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
(It will be said to them): “This is hell which the sinners had denied it.”
They will go around between it (hell) and the boiling hot water
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
But for those who fear the standing before their Lord, there will be 2 gardens (in Paradise)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
With spreading branches (of shady trees)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
In both of them 2 springs will be flowing
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
In both of them there will be every kind of fruit in pairs
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
They will recline on couches whose inner livings will be of silk brocade and the fruits of the 2 gardens will be near at hand
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Therein will be chaste virgins restraining their glances (upon their husbands only) whom no human or jinn has touched them before
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
They are (in beauty) like rubies and coral
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Is there any reward for good other than good
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Besides these 2 there shall be 2 other gardens (in Paradise)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
(shaded with) dark green (trees)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
In both of them there will be 2 springs gushing out water
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
In each of them there will be fruits, date-palms, and pomegranates
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Therein will be chaste and beautiful (virgins)
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Beautiful virgins (Huris) guarded in pavilions
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Whom no human or jinn has touched them before
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Reclining on green cushions and rich beautiful mattresses
Then which of your Lord’s favors will you both (jinns and human) deny
Blessed is the name of your Lord (Allah), the Owner of Majesty and Honor
When the event (the Day of Resurrection) will befall
there will be no denying of its befalling
it will bring low (to some), it will exalt (for others)
When the earth will be shaken with a terrible shake
and the mountains will be powdered to dust
so that they will become floating dust particles
And then you all will be in 3 kinds (separate groups)
those on the right hand (receive their records in right hands) who will be those on the right hand (will go to Paradise)
and those on the left hand (receive their records in left hands) who will be those on the left hand (will go to hell)
and those foremost (in Islamic faith) will be foremost (in Paradise)
Those will be nearest (to Allah)
in the gardens of delight (Paradise)
A most of them will be from the first generations (who embraced Islam)
and a few will be from the later generations
(They will be) on thrones of gold and precious stones
reclining on them face to face
immortal youths will go round serving them
with cups, jugs, and glasses of flowing wine
from where they will neither get any pain of the head, nor they will get any intoxication
(They will have) fruits of their own choice
and the flesh of fowls that they may desire
and Huris (chaste virgins) with wide lovely eyes
like guarded pearls
as a reward for what they used to do (good deeds)
They will neither hear any vain talk therein nor any sinful speech
but the saying of Salam! Salam! (greetings with peace)
And those on the right hand who will be those on the right hand
(They will be) among thornless lote-trees
and among banana trees with fruits piled one above another
and in long-extended shade
and by water flowing constantly
and fruit in plenty
whose season is not limited and their supply will not be cut off
and on high raised couches or thrones
Surely, We have created them (maidens) of special creation
and made them virgins
loving (their husbands only), equal in age
for those on the right hand
A large number will be from the first generation (who embraced Islam)
and a large number will be from the later generations
And those on the left hand - will be those on the left hand
(They will be) in fierce hot wind and boiling water
and in the shadow of black smoke
