On that Day, hearts will beat (with fear and anxiety)
their eyes will be downcast
They (disbelievers) say: “Shall we really be returned to the former state of life
when we will become crumbled bones?”
They say: “In that case, it would be a return with loss!”
But it will be only a single shout (the second blowing of the trumpet)
when they will be awakened (alive after death)
Have you heard the story of Moses
When his Lord called him in the sacred valley of Tuwa
and said: “Go to Pharaoh, surely he has transgressed all bounds
and say to him: ‘Do you have the desire to purify yourself (from sins)
I will guide you to your Lord, so that you may fear (Him).’”
Then he (Moses) showed him (Pharaoh) the great sign (miracles)
but he (Pharaoh) denied and disobeyed
Then he turned his back and strive (against Allah)
gathered his people and cried aloud
saying: “I am your Lord, most high.”
So Allah seized him with punishment for the Hereafter and this life
Surely, in this, there is an admonition for those who fear (Allah)
Are you (O mankind) more difficult to create or the heaven that He constructed
He raised its canopy and perfected it
He covers its night with darkness and brings out light in its forenoon
And after that, He spreads out the earth
and brings out its water and its pasture from there
fixed the mountains firmly
made a provision and benefit for you and for your cattle
But when the greatest catastrophe (the Day of recompense) will strike
the Day when people will remember what they had striven for
When hellfire shall be made apparent in full view for those who see
then, those who transgressed all bounds (evil deeds)
and preferred the worldly life
surely, will have their abode in hell
But those who feared standing before their Lord and restrained themselves from evil desires
then surely, will have their homes in Paradise
They ask you (O Muhammad) about the Hour: “When will be its appointed time?”
But you have no knowledge to say anything about it
Only your Lord (has knowledge of) the term of it
You (O Muhammad) are only a Warner for those who fear it
On that Day, when they will see it, it will be as if they had not stayed (in this world) only an afternoon or one morning
He (the prophet) frowned and turned away
when there came to him the blind man (Abdullah bin Umme Maktoom, who came to the prophet while the prophet was preaching to the chiefs of Makkah)
And how can you know? He might become pure (from sins)
or he might receive admonition, and the admonition might profit him
As for those who think themselves indifferent
to whom you were attending
you will not be held responsible, if they would not purify themselves (your duty is to convey the message of Allah)
Yet, to him who came to you running (with enthusiasm)
and with fear (of Allah)
you were unmindful from him
Nay, (you should not do so), indeed this is an admonition
so those who want, let them pay attention to it
It is written in honored records
exalted (in dignity), purified
in the hands of scribes (angels)
(who are) honorable and obedient
Be cursed (disbelieving) people! How ungrateful they are
Out of what He has created them
From semen drop He has created them and then set them in due proportion
then makes their way (of life) easy for them
then causes them to die and puts them in their graves
Then, He will surely resurrect them again when He wills
Nay, but they (disbelievers) have not fulfilled what He has commanded them
Then let people look at their food
We pour out water (rain) in abundance
then split the earth (soil) in clefts
And We cause to grow in it the grain
and grapes and clover plants
and olives and date-palms
and gardens, dense with many trees
and fruits and fodder
as a provision and benefit for you and your cattle
Then when there will come the deafening shout
on that Day a person will flee from his brother
and his mother and his father
and his spouse and its children
On that Day, every person will have enough concern to become careless of others
Some faces on that Day will be bright (for true believers)
laughing, rejoicing at good news (of Paradise)
And other faces on that Day will be dusty
darkness will cover them
Such will be the (faces of the) disbelieving wicked
When the sun will cease to shine (overthrown)
and when the stars will fall
and when the mountains will be moved away
and when the pregnant she-camels will be neglected (unattended)
and when the wild beasts will be gathered together
and when the seas will overflow (or set on fire)
and when the souls will be joined (with their bodies)
and when the infant girl buried alive (as the pagan Arabs used to do) will be questioned
for what sin she was killed
and when the written pages (record of deeds) will be laid open
and when the heaven will be stripped off (taken away from its place)
and when hellfire will be kindled to blaze (fierce heat)
and when Paradise will be brought near
then every person will know what he has brought (of good and evil)
So surely, I swear by the planets that recede
and that move swiftly and hide themselves
and by the night as it departs
and by the dawn as it brightens
surely, this is the Word (this Qur’an) of a honorable Messenger (Gabriel from Allah to Muhammad)
possessor of mighty power, established (high rank) with the Owner of the Throne (Allah)
obeyed (by the angels in the heaven), and trustworthy
(O people of Makkah) your companion (Muhammad) is not a mad man
and indeed he (Muhammad) saw him (Gabriel) in the clear horizon
and he (Muhammad) does not withhold knowledge on the unseen
And this (Qur’an) is not the word of the outcast Satan
Then where are you going
This (the Qur’an) is but a reminder to the people of the worlds
to whoever among you who wishes to follow the Right Way
Yet, you will not (avail your wishes) unless that Allah wills, the Lord of the worlds
When the heaven will cleft asunder
and when the stars will scatter
and when the oceans are burst out
and when the graves will be turned upside down (bring out their contents)
every person will know what he has sent forward and what left behind
O people! What has made you careless about your Lord, the Generous
who created you, fashioned you perfectly, gave you due proportion
and put you together in whatever form He willed
Nay! But you deny the Day of Judgment
But surely, (angels have been appointed to watch) over you
(who are) honorable writers
they know all of what you do
Surely, (on that Day) the righteous will be in delight (Paradise)
and surely, the wicked (evil-doers) will be in the fire (hell)
and they will burn in it on the Day of recompense
and they will not be able to escape from it
And what will make you know what the Day of the recompense is
Again, what will make you know what the Day of recompense is
(It will be) the Day when no one will have the power to do anything for another: on that Day, the decision will be entirely with Allah
Woe to those who give less in measure and weight (defraud)
those who, when they receive by measure from people, demand full measure
but when they give by measure or give by weight to others, they give less than due
Don’t they think that they will be resurrected
on a great Day
the Day when all mankind will stand before the Lord of the worlds
Nay! Truly, the record of the deeds of the wicked is (preserved) in prison register (Sijjin)
and what will make you know what Sijjin is
A register inscribed (of hell)
Woe on that Day to those who deny (disbelievers)
who deny the Day of recompense
None can deny it except every transgressor beyond bounds, the sinner
When Our Verses (of the Qur’an) are recited to them, they say: “Tales of the ancients!”
Nay! But their sins and evil deeds which they used to earn have caused a covering on their hearts
Nay! Surely, on that Day, they (evil-doers) will be veiled from (the vision of) their Lord
Then, surely they will indeed burn in the hell
and it will be said to them: “This is what you used to deny!”
Nay! Surely, the record of the righteous deeds is indeed (preserved) in register of exalted ones (Illiyun)
and what will make you know what Illiyun is
A register inscribed (of Paradise)
bears witness of those who are nearest (to Allah, i.e. the angels)
Surely, the righteous will be in delight (Paradise)
on thrones, looking (at all things)
you will recognize in their faces the brightness of delight
They will be given to drink from pure sealed wine
the seal of that wine will be smell of musk. Those who want to strive, let them strive
That (wine) will be a mixture of Tasnim
a spring where those nearest to Allah will drink
Surely! Those who committed crimes (in this world), used to laugh at those who believed
and wink one to another (in mockery) whenever they passed by them
When they returned to their own people, they would return joking
When they saw them (believers), they used to say: “Surely! These people have indeed gone astray,”
though they (disbelievers) had not been sent over them (believers) as watchers
On that Day (the Day of Resurrection) the believers will laugh at the disbelievers
as they recline on high couches and look (at then saying)
“Are not the disbelievers rewarded for what they used to do?”
When the heaven will split asunder
listens to and obeys its Lord and it must do so
And when the earth will stretch out
and cast out all that is in it and becomes empty
listens and obeys to its Lord and it must do so
O mankind! Surely, you must strive very hard towards your Lord; then you will meet (Allah)
Then those who will be given their record (of deeds) in their right hand
surely they will receive easy reckoning
and will return to their family in joy
But those who will be given their record (deeds) from behind their back
will invoke for destruction
and shall burn in a blazing fire
for they used to live among their people in joy
and thought that they would never come back (to Us for accounts)
Yes! Surely, their Lord was watching (over their misdeeds)
So I swear by the glow of sunset
and by the night and whatever it gathers in its darkness
and by the moon when it grows full
that you will certainly travel from stage to stage (this life and the Hereafter)
What is the matter with the people that they don’t believe
and when the Qur’an is recited to them, they don’t prostrate
Nay, the disbelievers will deny (Islam)
and Allah knows best what they are hiding (in their hearts)
So, announce to them, a painful punishment
except those who believe and do good deeds; for them there will be a never ending reward (Paradise)
By the heaven holding the big stars
And by the Promised Day (of judgment)
And by the witnesses and that which is being witnessed
Cursed be the people of the ditch
who lit the fire fed with fuel
and they sat by it (fire)
to watch what they were doing to the believers
And they took revenge on them for no other reason except that they believed in Allah, the All-Mighty, the Praise-worthy
to whom belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth! And Allah is witness over everything
Surely, those who persecute the believing men and believing women and don’t repent (to Allah), then they will receive the punishment of hell and they will have the punishment of the burning fire
Surely, those who believe and do righteous deeds, they will have gardens under which rivers flow (Paradise). That is the great success
Surely, (O Muhammad) the grip (punishment) of your Lord is very severe
Surely, it is He Who originates (created everything) and will repeat it (on the Day of Resurrection)
Allah is Forgiving, the Loving (to the pious)
the Owner of the Throne, the Glorious
and (He) does whatever He intends (or wills)
Has the story reached you of the hosts
of Pharaoh and Thamud
Nay! The disbelievers (persist) in denying (the truth)
and Allah has encompassed them from all around
Nay! This is a Glorious Qur’an
(inscribed) in the preserved tablet (Al-Lauh Al-Mahfuz)
By the heaven and the night-comer (the bright star)
and what will make you know what night-comer is
(It is) the star of piercing brightness
There is no human being but has a protector (angel) over him
So let a person see from what he is created
He is created from an emitted fluid
that is produced from between the back-bone and the ribs
Surely, (Allah) is Able to bring a person back (to life)
on the Day when all the secrets will be examined
he will have neither power, nor any helper (to save from punishment)
By the sky (with rain clouds) with the returning rain (again and again)
and by the earth which splits (for springs or growth of trees and plants)
surely! this (Qur’an) is the Word that separates (truth from falsehood)
and it is not for amusement
These (unbelievers) are plotting a plot (against you O Muhammad)
and I too am plotting a plan
Give respite to the disbelievers. Give respite to them gently (for a while)
Glorify the name of your Lord, the High
Who has created everything, and then proportioned them
Who has measured (destinies) and then guided them
Who brings out the pasture (vegetation eaten by animals)
then makes it dark rubbish
We shall make you recite (the Qur’an) so you (O Muhammad) shall not forget it
except what Allah wills. Surely He knows what is open and what is hidden
And We shall make it easy for you (O Muhammad) to follow the easy way (to do righteous deeds)
Therefore remind, surely, reminder does benefit
Whoever fears (Allah) will heed the reminder
and the wretched will avoid it
who will burn in the great fire
where he will neither die in it nor live (a good living)
Indeed whoever purifies himself shall achieve success
and who remembers the Name of his Lord and prays
Nay, (O people) you prefer the worldly life
although the Hereafter is better and everlasting
Surely! This is in the former Scriptures
the Scriptures of Abraham and Moses
Has the news of the overwhelming event (of Resurrection) reached you
On that Day some faces will be humiliated (in the hellfire)
in hard labor, worn out
burn in the hot blazing fire
given to drink from a boiling spring
They will have no food except bitter thorny fruit
that will neither nourish nor satisfy hunger
Other faces on that Day will be joyful
pleased with their endeavors (of good deeds)
in a high garden (Paradise)
They will hear no vain talk in it
They will have a running spring in it
They will be on thrones raised high in it
with cups placed at hand
and cushions set in rows
and rich carpets spread out
Don’t they look at the camels, how they are created
And the sky, how it is raised
And the mountains, how they are fixed firmly
And the earth, how it is spread out
So remind them (O Muhammad), you are only a reminder
not a dictator over them
Except those who turn away and disbelieve
then Allah will punish them with the greatest punishment
Surely, to Us will be their return
then surely, We will take their reckoning
By the dawn
by the 10 nights (first 10 days of the month of Dhul-Hijja)
by the even and the odd (of all the creations of Allah)
and by the night when it departs
Are there not in them (above oaths) sufficient proofs for the people of understanding
Have you (O Muhammad) not seen how your Lord dealt with Ad (people)
(Tall residents of) Iram with lofty pillars
the like of which were not created like them in the land
With Thamud (people), who cut out rocks in the valley (to make residences)
With Pharaoh who had the stakes
They all transgressed beyond bounds in the lands
and made much mischief in it
So your Lord poured on them different kinds of punishment
Surely, your Lord is ever watchful (over them)
As for people, when their Lord tries them and gives them honor and bounties, they say: “Our Lord has honored us.”
But when He tries them through restricting their means of life, then they say: “Our Lord has humiliated us!”
Nay! But you did not treat the orphans with kindness and generosity
nor did you encourage each other in feeding the poor
You devour inheritance (of the weak) with greed
and you love wealth with much love
Nay! When the earth will be grounded to exceeding grinding (powder)
your Lord will come with the angels standing in rows
hell will be brought near (in sight) that Day. On that Day people will remember (their deeds), but how the remembrance will avail them
One will say: “Alas! Would that I had sent forth (good deeds) for my life?”
On that Day, none will punish anymore except His punishment
and none can bind anyone like His binding
(It will be said to the pious): “O you the one in satisfaction
Come back to your Lord, well-pleased and well-pleasing (to Him)
Then you enter among My servants
and you enter My Paradise!”
I swear by this city (Makkah, where it is prohibited to harm anyone)
you (O Muhammad) are free (from sin to punish the enemies of Islam) in this city (Makkah)
and by the father (Adam) and the children which he begot (mankind)
surely, We have created human in toil (to work hard)
Does human think that none can overcome them
Human says (boastfully): “I have wasted wealth in abundance!”
Does human thinks that none sees them
Have We not made for them a pair of eyes (to see)
And a tongue and a pair of lips (to control)
And shown him the 2 ways (good and evil)
Yet, human has not attempted to pass on the steep path (Aqabah)
And what will make you know what the steep path is
(It is) the freeing of a neck (slave from bondage)
or giving food in a day of hunger (famine)
to an orphan relative
or to a poor clinging to dust (out of misery)
then human should be one of those who believe, recommend one another to the patience, and recommend one another to kindness and compassion
They are the people of the Right Hand (people of Paradise)
But those who disbelieve in Our revelations, they are the people of the left hand (people of hell)
with the fire all around them
By the sun and its brightness
by the moon as it follows it (sun)
by the day as it shows up (the sun’s) brightness
by the night as it conceals it (the sun)
by the heaven and Him who built it
by the earth and Him who spread it
by the soul and Him who perfected it in proportion
and He inspired him with (knowledge of) what is wrong for him and what is right for him
Indeed one will succeed who purifies his own self (obey Allah)
and indeed one will fail who corrupts him (disobey Allah)
Thamud (people) denied (their prophet) through their transgression (by rejecting the truth)
when the most wicked person among them went out (to kill the she-camel)
The Messenger of Allah (Saleh) said to them: “That is the she-camel of Allah! (Don’t harm it and don’t stop it from) its drink.”
They denied him and killed her. So their Lord destroyed them because of their sin, and made them equal in destruction (leveled to ground)
And He has no fear of its consequences
By the night, when it covers (with darkness)
and by the day, when it appears in brightness
By Him Who created the male and the female
surely, your efforts are indeed diverse (different purpose)
As for the one who gives (in charity), fears Him
and believes in the best (deed)
We will make smooth for him (the path) of ease
As for the one who is miser and thinks itself self-sufficient
and denies the best (deed)
We will make smooth for him (the path) for evil
Think! what its wealth will benefit when one goes down (doomed)
Surely! (It is) on Us to give guidance
and surely, to Us belong the last (Hereafter) and the first (this world)
Therefore, I warn you of the blazing fire (of hell)
In which none will burn except the most wretched
who denies (the truth) and turns away
But the pious will be far removed from it (hell)
the one who spends his wealth (in charity) that may grow (for self-purification)
who has in mind no favor from anyone to be paid back
except to seek the pleasure of his Lord, the High
Such person will be pleased (with Allah when he will enter Paradise)
By the morning day light
and by the night when it covers (with darkens)
(O Muhammad) your Lord has neither forsaken you nor displeased with you
Indeed, the Hereafter will be better for you than the first (worldly life)
Surely, your Lord will give you (good) so that you will be well-pleased
Did He not find you (O Muhammad) an orphan and gave you a refuge
And did He not find you (O Muhammad) lost and gave you guidance
And did He not find you (O Muhammad) poor and made you rich (self-sufficient)
So, don’t treat the orphan with oppression
and don’t repulse the beggar
and proclaim the Grace of your Lord
Have We not opened your heart for you (O Muhammad)
and removed your burden from you
which weighed down your back
and raised high for you your fame
Surely, with the hardship, there is relief
Surely, with the hardship, there is relief
When you have finished (your work), then stand up (for Allah’s worship)
and turn (your attention) to your Lord
By the fig and by the olive
by the mount of Sinai
and by this city of security (Makkah)
Surely, We have created people in the best stature
then We will reduce it to the lowest of the low
except those who believe (in Islam) and do righteous deeds, then for them will be a reward without end (Paradise)
So, what causes you (disbelievers) to deny about the Day of Judgment
Is not Allah the best of the judges
Read! In the name of your Lord, who has created (everything)
created human from a clot (thick blood)
Read! Your Lord is the Generous
who has taught (writing) by the pen
taught human what it did not know
Nay! Surely, human does transgress
because it considers itself self-sufficient
surely, to your Lord is the return
Have you seen him (Abu Jahl) who prevents
a servant (Muhammad) from offering prays
Have you seen if he (Muhammad) is on the guidance (of Allah)
or enjoins piety
Have you seen if he (Abu Jahl) denies (truth) and turn away
Does he (Abu Jahl) not know that Allah sees (everything)
Nay! If he (Abu Jahl) does not stop, We will catch him by the forelock
a lying, sinful forelock
So let him call his council (of help)
We will call out the guards of hell (to deal with him)
Nay! (O Muhammad)! Don’t obey him (Abu Jahl). Prostrate and draw near (to Allah)
Surely! We have sent this (Qur’an) down in the night of Decree (Qadr)
What will make you understand what the night of Decree (Qadr) is
The night of Decree is better than 1,000 months
The angels and the spirit (Gabriel) descend at that night by the permission of their Lord with all Decrees
(All that night) there is peace till the appearance of dawn
Those who disbelieve from among the people of the Scripture and from the polytheists were not going to leave (from their disbelief) until clear evidence came to them
a Messenger from Allah reciting from the purified pages
containing correct and right laws (in Scriptures)
And those who were given the Scripture did not differ until after clear evidence (this Qur’an) came to them
And they were commanded nothing but to worship Allah with their sincere devotion to Him, being upright (true in their faith); to establish prayer, to pay obligatory charity; and that is the right religion
Surely, those who disbelieve from among the people of the Scripture and the polytheists will be in the fire of hell. They will abide in it forever. They are the worst of all creatures
Surely, those who believe and do righteous deeds, they are the best of all creatures
Their reward with their Lord shall be the gardens of Eden (eternity), beneath which rivers flow, they will abide in it forever. Allah will be pleased with them and they will be pleased with Him. That is for those who fear their Lord
When the earth will be shaken with its (final) earthquake
and when the earth will throw out its inner burdens
and people will say: “What is the matter with it?”
On that Day it will declare whatever had happened (to it)
because your Lord will command it
On that Day, mankind will proceed in sorted groups so that they may be shown their (book of) deeds
Whoever has done good equal to the weight of an atom, shall see it there
whoever has done evil equal to the weight of an atom, shall see it there
By the (steeds) that run with panting (breath)
striking sparks of fire (by their hoops)
making raids in the morning
leaving a trail of dust in it
as they penetrate directly into the middle (of the enemy)
Surely! Human is ungrateful to his Lord
and verily, he bears witness to it (by his deeds)
and surely, he is violent in the love of wealth
He does not know when the contents of the graves will be brought out (resurrected)
and that which is in the hearts (of people) will be made known
surely, on that Day (of Resurrection) their Lord will be well-acquainted with them
The striking Hour (Qari’ah, the Day of Calamity)
What is the striking Hour
What will make you know what the striking Hour is
It is the Day when mankind will be like scattered moths
and the mountains will be like carded wool
then as for the one whose balance (of good deeds) will be heavy
he will reside in a pleasant life (Paradise)
But as for the one whose balance (of good deeds) will be light
he will abode in hell (Hawiyah)
and what will make you know what it (Hawiyah) is
(It is) a blazing fire
(O mankind) you are distracted by the mutual rivalry (of piling up of worldly gains)
(never be satisfied) until you come to the graves (die)
Nay! You will soon come to know
Again, Nay! You will soon come to know
Nay! If you knew with real knowledge (from Qur’an)
Surely, You will see the blazing fire (of hell)
and you will see it with certainty of sight
then, on that Day, you shall be questioned about the blessings (given in the world and how you used)
By the time (through the ages)
Surely! Mankind is in loss
except those who believe and do righteous deeds; exhort one another to the truth and exhort one another to patience
Woe to every slanderer and backbiter
who gathers wealth and counts it
One who thinks that his wealth will make him last forever
Nay! Surely, he will be thrown into the crushing fire
What will make you know what the crushing fire is
The fire kindled by Allah
The one who will leap up over the hearts
surely, it will close on them (from all sides)
in outstretched pillars (of fire)
Have you (O Muhammad) not seen how your Lord dealt with the owners of the elephant (The elephant army came under the command of Abraha, king of Yemen, who intended to destroy the Ka’bah at Makkah in the year of Muhammad’s year of birth)
Did He not make their plot go in astray
And He sent against them birds in flocks
which pelted them with stones of baked clay
and He made them like the chewed-up stalks
(It is a great blessing and protection from Allah) for the safety of Quraish (caretaker of the house of Allah)
for the safe passage (of their trade caravans) in winter and summer
So let them worship the Lord of this house (the Ka’bah in Makkah)
who provided them food against hunger and made them safe against fear
Have you seen the one who denies the Day of Judgment
It is he who drives away the orphan (harshly)
and don’t encourage the feeding of the poor
So woe to those who perform prayers (hypocrites)
but are heedless of their prayer
those who do good deeds only to be seen
and they refuge (to share) small kindnesses
Surely, We have granted you (Muhammad) a river in Paradise (Kauther)
Therefore, offer prayer to your Lord and sacrifice
Surely, he who hates you (O Muhammad), he will be cut off (from good of both worlds)
Say (O Muhammad): “O disbelievers
‘I don’t worship that whom you worship
nor will you worship that whom I worship
I will never worship those (deities) whom you worship
nor will you ever worship (Allah) whom I worship
to you be your religion, and to me my religion (Islam).’”
When there comes the Help of Allah (to you, O Muhammad against your enemies) and the victory (of Makkah)
and you see the people entering in Allah’s religion (Islam) in crowds
So glorify the praises of your Lord, and ask for His forgiveness. Surely, He is the one who accepts repentance (and forgives)
Perish the 2 hands of Abu Lahab (uncle of the prophet) and perish him
His wealth and whatever he earned did not benefit him
He will be burnt soon in a fire of blazing flames
and his wife, the carrier of wood (she used to put thorns on the way of the prophet)
she will have a twisted rope of palm fiber around her neck
Say (O Muhammad): “He is Allah, (the) One
Allah is the Self-Sufficient (Samad: independent of all, while all are dependent on Allah)
He begets not, nor is He begotten
and there is none comparable to Him.”
Say: “I seek refuge with the Lord of the Daybreak
from the evil of what He has created
and from the evil of the darkness (night) as it comes with its darkness
and from the evil of the witches who blow in the knots (black magic)
and from the evil of the envier when one envies.”
Say: “I seek refuge with the Lord of mankind
the Owner of mankind
the real One worthy of worship of mankind
from the evil of the sneaking whispers (Satan and its workers)
who whispers into the hearts of people
from (among) the jinns and mankind.”
